<section>
<section.front>
<outline.name.block>
<label>&sect;</label>
<designator>10:2</designator>
<name>Form and procedure</name>
</outline.name.block>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
Judgments and final orders, as well as the orders in this chapter that are not final, contain a caption in the form of the action, a designation as the appropriate judgment or order, a commencement that sometimes includes findings of fact and a body that contains the adjudications made by the judgment or order. See <x>&sect;2:2; st.ref.id="I03XWRW">Fla. R. Civ. P. 1.100(c); <field>st.ref.id="I015V9P"</field>Fla. Fam. L. R. P. 12.100(c). Judgments and orders are completed by a conclusion that gives the date and place of entry and the signature of the judge. A notation of the parties or attorneys to whom conformed copies of the judgment have been sent is in the lower left-hand part of the form.
</x>
</para.text>
</para>
<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
After a judgment is entered, it must be filed with the clerk, and recorded. If it is not a final judgment or order, it may be recorded if the court so orders. Interlocutory orders that deal with the title to or possession of real property should always be recorded.
</para.text>
</para>
<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
The commencement of final judgments differs. There is one form for an application for judgment after default, others for judgment after motion for judgment on the pleadings, for summary judgment, for dismissal and for jury trials and nonjury trials. The commencement should recite the predicate for its entry, such as one of the motions, a jury or nonjury trial, and then move on to the adjudicatory paragraphs. Most lawyers call the judgment after a motion for summary judgment a summary judgment. It is not. It is a final judgment granted after a motion for summary judgment. It can properly be called a summary final judgment, but it is better to call it simply a final judgment.
</para.text>
</para>
<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
The commencement must contain findings of fact in some cases.<trace> </trace><trace></trace><trace>The failure to include the required findings of fact in </trace><trace>a</trace><trace> final judgment</trace><trace> leave the judgment open to attack by rehearing, appeal, and ultimately a new trial</trace><trace>. </trace><trace></trace><trace>See Fla. R. Civ. P. 1.530</trace><trace> and Fam. L. R. P. 12.530.</trace>
</para.text>
</para>
<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
st.ref.id="I02T6UB">Rule 1.560(c) of the Florida Rules of Civil Procedure was amended to authorize a requirement that a judgment debtor furnish a fact information sheet to the judgment creditor's attorney. See <field>st.ref.id="I05VWWO"</field>Fla. R. Civ. P. Form 1.977. The form may be subject to challenge in requiring a nonparty spouse to divulge separate property. A similar requirement form is authorized for small claims. See <field>st.ref.id="I052Z2G"</field>Fla. Sm. Cl. R. 7.221. The provision for the requirement is in <x>&sect;10:13. It can be added to any other form to which it is applicable.
</x>
</para.text>
</para>
<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
Costs are included in all of the forms of final judgments. Many times court costs cannot be awarded when judgment is entered so a motion to tax costs must be filed and a separate order taxing costs entered. See <x>&sect;7:<trace>200</trace><trace.deleted/>&sect;<trace.deleted/>; <x>&sect;7:201; <x>&sect;7:30<trace>5</trace><trace.deleted/>.
</x>
</para.text>
</para>
<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
For a money judgment to become a lien on the judgment debtor's property it must contain the prevailing party's address and the non-prevailing party's address and Social Security number if known or an affidavit must be recorded with the information at the same time as the certified copy of the judgment.
</para.text>
</para>
<item.reference.block>
<item.reference>
<name.block>
<label>Author's</label>
<designator>&lsqb;'Comment'&rsqb;</designator>
</name.block></item.reference></item.reference.block>
<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|2|10:2">
<para.text>
See st.ref.id="I02T71J">&sect;28.222(3)(c), Fla. Stat.; <field>st.ref.id="I02T776"</field>&sect;28.29, Fla. Stat. See <field>cc.ref.id="I05QEGP"</field>Sun Bank/Southwest, N.A. v. Schad, 482 So. 2d 554 (Fla. 2d DCA 1986) for the immediate issuance of the execution; and <field>cc.ref.id="I05NLHH"</field>Robinson v. Sterling Door &amp; Window Co., Inc., 698 So. 2d 570 (Fla. 1st DCA 1997) for the requirement of the parties' addresses and the judgment debtor's party's Social Security number for money judgments. See <field>st.ref.id="I05VWI9"</field>&sect;55.10(2), Fla. Stat.
</para.text>
</para>
</section.body>

</form.text>
</form.para>

Petitioner contends that the City refused the rezoning petition because of the political pressure brought by the number of opponents of the rezoning request who were present at the public hearing. Petitioner did not have a court reporter present and the record from the electronic recording machines is so poor that the events transpiring at the hearing cannot be determined with certainty. Since there is an inadequate record of the proceedings below from which it can be determined that the City erred as a matter of law.

<form uuid="I7b00f4d09fed11dfbf230000837214a9">
<caption.block ref=manual date.updated="0">
<form.line align = "c">IN THE CIRCUIT COURT FOR &lsqb;NAME OF COUNTY&rsqb;, FLORIDA</form.line>

        <row><entry style="block" resize="same"></entry><entry colname="2" style="block" resize="same">Petitioner,</entry><entry style="block" resize="same"></entry></row>

<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<form.text>
This action seeks a writ of certiorari to the County Court of <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of county&rsqb;</inline.instr>, Florida, to review a discovery order. Petitioner in this action is plaintiff in the county court and seeks damages for breach of contract. Defendant counterclaimed for malicious interference. Defendant propounded interrogatories seeking information about plaintiff's assets, liabilities, customer names and other financial information. The pleadings do not seek punitive damages at this stage and no discovery has been conducted as contemplated by st.ref.id="I05Q5XJ">&sect;768.72 Florida Statutes as a predicate for amending to plead punitive damages.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<form.text>
Plaintiff objected to interrogatories <inline.instr>&lsqb;designation of interrogatories&rsqb;</inline.instr> that seek financial and business information on the grounds that customers' names were a trade secret and financial information was not relevant. The county court overruled the objections and ordered plaintiff to provide the requested discovery.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<form.text>
Defendant supports the county court order on the grounds that it may lead to admissible evidence and provide the basis for punitive damages. Plaintiff contends that discovery on that basis is premature.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<form.text>
The court finds that the interrogatories are premature, except interrogatory 16 seeking customer names, so
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<form.text>
IT IS ADJUDGED that:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<form.text>
Certiorari is granted and the order of the County Court of &lsqb;name of county&rsqb;, Florida dated &lsqb;date of order&rsqb; overruling plaintiff's objections to defendant's interrogatories is quashed, except for interrogatory &lsqb;designation of interrogatory&rsqb;.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<form.text>
This action is remanded to the County Court of &lsqb;name of county&rsqb;, Florida for further proceedings consistent with this judgment.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|9|10:9">
<form.text>
Petitioner &lsqb;NAME OF PLAINTIFF&rsqb;, whose address is &lsqb;address of petitioner&rsqb;, recover from &lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT&rsqb; &lsqb;OPTIONAL:, whose address is &lsqb;address of defendant&rsqb; and the last four digits of Social Security number are &lsqb;last four numbers of Social Security number&rsqb;,&rsqb; the sum of $&lsqb;dollar amount of costs&rsqb; for costs that shall bear interest at the rate prescribed by law, for which let execution issue forthwith.

</form.text>
</form.para>

Petitioner &lsqb;NAME OF PLAINTIFF&rsqb;, whose address is &lsqb;address of petitioner&rsqb;, recover from &lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT&rsqb; &lsqb;OPTIONAL:, whose address is &lsqb;address of defendant&rsqb; and the last four digits of Social Security number are &lsqb;last four numbers of Social Security number&rsqb;,&rsqb; the sum of $&lsqb;dollar amount of costs&rsqb; for costs that shall bear interest at the rate prescribed by law, for which let execution issue forthwith.

<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|14|10:14">
<form.text>
This action was tried before the court. On the evidence presented
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|14|10:14">
<form.text>
IT IS ADJUDGED that:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|14|10:14">
<form.text>
Defendant did not construct the apartment building as specified by the drawings and specifications in the following particulars:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(a)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|14|10:14">
<form.text>
The concrete in the grade beams and columns was not of the strength specified, testing at less than half the required strength;
</form.text>
</form.para>
</form.item>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(b)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|14|10:14">
<form.text>
The interior drywall was exposed to the elements before installation with resulting deterioration so that it buckled and would not take wallpaper;
</form.text>
</form.para>
</form.item>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(c)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|14|10:14">
<form.text>
Aluminum electrical wiring was installed instead of copper.
</form.text>
</form.para>
</form.item>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|14|10:14">
<form.text>
The completion of the building was delayed by 187 days. The contractor is responsible for 92 days of delay. The remaining delay was caused by the failure of the architect to prepare the drawings and specification in accordance with the Standard Building Code and to promptly process change orders.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|14|10:14">
<form.text>
Plaintiff did not pay defendant at the times required by the contract documents. The delays in timely payments caused damages to defendant of $67,258.19 in lost discounts, interest on delayed payments and disruption of defendant's operations on the project.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|14|10:14">
<form.text>
Defendant's delay in completion, disregarding the delays caused by the architect, caused plaintiff to lose $30,000 in rent.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|14|10:14">
<form.text>
Change orders directed by plaintiff that have not been paid to defendant have a value of $110,516.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|14|10:14">
<form.text>
The apartment building was not substantially completed because of the defects listed in paragraph 1. Nevertheless, plaintiff elected to accept the building and sought an equitable reduction in the contract price. Plaintiff is entitled to a reduction of $180,500 for the defects.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|14|10:14">
<form.text>
Defendant's surety is jointly and severally liable with defendant to plaintiff under the performance bond for the failure to perform the contract. The surety is not liable under the payment bond for reimbursement to plaintiff for amounts paid to discharge construction liens because the bond contains a condition precedent that plaintiff pay progress payments in accordance with the contract documents. Plaintiff did not do so as adjudged in paragraph 3.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|14|10:14">
<form.text>
Defendant and the surety are liable to plaintiff for $32,725.81.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|14|10:14">
<form.text>
Jurisdiction is reserved to award supplemental relief and attorney fees and to tax costs.
</form.text>

<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|17|10:17">
<form.text>
This action was heard on plaintiff's motion for a deficiency judgment. On the evidence presented,

</form.para>

<form.text>
IT IS ADJUDGED that plaintiff <inline.instr>&lsqb;NAME OF PLAINTIFF&rsqb;</inline.instr>, whose address is <inline.instr>&lsqb;address of plaintiff&rsqb;</inline.instr>, recover from defendant <inline.instr>&lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT&rsqb;</inline.instr> <inline.instr>&lsqb;OPTIONAL:, whose address is &lsqb;address of defendant&rsqb;</inline.instr> and the last four digits of Social Security number are <inline.instr>&lsqb;last four numbers of Social Security number&rsqb;</inline.instr>,&rsqb; the sum of $<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of judgment due&rsqb;</inline.instr> as the balance due on the final judgment entered in this action, $<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of interest&rsqb;</inline.instr> as interest from the date of the final judgment to the date of this deficiency judgment with costs of $<inline.instr>&lsqb;dollar amount of costs&rsqb;</inline.instr>, making a total of $<inline.instr>&lsqb;total dollar amount of judgment due&rsqb;</inline.instr>, that shall bear interest at the rate prescribed by law, for which let execution issue forthwith.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|17|10:17">

<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|17|10:17">
<form.text>
A deficiency judgment is a money judgment entered in a foreclosure action. If an attorney fee is given, this form must contain the requirements of cc.ref.id="I06RQ6I">Florida Patient's Compensation Fund v. Rowe, 472 So. 2d 1145 (Fla. 1985), holding modified by Standard Guar. Ins. Co. v. Quanstrom, 555 So. 2d 828 (Fla. 1990) or a reservation of jurisdiction to set the fee. See <x>&sect;10:13, Comment.

<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|18|10:18">
<form.text>
This form is a slightly different version of st.ref.id="I02T7TW">Florida Rules of Civil Procedure Form 1.994 in that it is designed for the dismissal of an extraordinary writ action. This form assumes the alternative writ was issued as required by Rule 1.630(d) or Rule 12.630(d). If the writ is granted the terminology would be peremptory writ shall be issued and defendant shall obey it. Ordinarily, a defendant in a mandamus action will have no assessable costs. See the exception for certiorari in <x>section 10:8. See <field>cc.ref.id="I03TU75"</field>Fla. R. Civ. P. 1.630; <field>cc.ref.id="I03WNC1"</field>Fla. Fam. L. R. P. 12.630; <field>st.ref.id="I0469QC"</field>Fla. R. Gen. Prac. &amp; Jud. Admin. 2.130.

<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|22|10:22">
</caption.block>
<form.text>
This action was tried before the court. On the evidence presented the court finds that the directors of <inline.instr>&lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT CORPORATION&rsqb;</inline.instr> are deadlocked in the management of the corporate affairs and the shareholders are unable to break the deadlock. As a result irreparable injury to the corporate defendant's assets is now being suffered and unless the action taken under this final judgment occurs, the assets will be lost to the shareholders. The corporation has complied with st.ref.id="I04BHVZ">&sect;607.1431(4), Fla. Stat., however the shareholders have not elected to purchase the plaintiff's shares, therefore
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|22|10:22">
<form.text>
IT IS ADJUDGED that:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|22|10:22">
<form.text>
Defendant &lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT CORPORATION&rsqb; is dissolved effective &lsqb;date of dissolution&rsqb;.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|22|10:22">
<form.text>
The directors shall sell all of the assets of the corporation as soon as possible. When sufficient assets are sold so that all creditors can be paid, the directors of the corporation shall pay the debts of the corporation.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|22|10:22">
<form.text>
If there is an excess of funds after the debts of the corporation are paid, the balance after paying the debts of the corporation shall be paid to the stockholders of the corporation pro rata according to the amounts of stock owned by each.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|22|10:22">
<form.text>
The directors of the corporation shall follow the procedures prescribed by &dblsect;607.1406 and 607.1407, Florida Statutes as may be necessary to dispose of all claims against the corporation by its creditors.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|22|10:22">
<form.text>
The court reserves jurisdiction of the corporation to enforce this judgment and to enter any other orders that may be necessary for the complete and proper disposition of the corporation's assets.
</form.text>

<outline.name.block>
<label>&sect;</label>
<designator>10:29</designator>
<name>Judgment<sep/> Ejectment, betterment</name>
</outline.name.block>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|29|10:29">
<para.text>
The form for the prevailing party will be a judgment for money. See <x>&sect;10:13. The prevailing party is determined by the mathematics required by st.ref.id="I04AC7L">&sect;66.061, Fla. Stat. Judgment is then rendered for the party receiving the balance. See also <field>st.ref.id="I01SU5J"</field>&sect;66.091, Fla. Stat.; &sect;66.101, Fla. Stat. (payment options); <x>&sect;9:23 (the verdict).
</x>
</para.text>
</para>
</section.body>

</form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
Plaintiff &lsqb;NAME OF PLAINTIFF&rsqb;, whose address is &lsqb;address of plaintiff&rsqb;, is due $&lsqb;dollar amount of improvements&rsqb; for labor, services and material furnished to improve the real property described in paragraph 2, $&lsqb;dollar amount of interest&rsqb; as interest to the date of this judgment, with costs of $&lsqb;dollar amount of costs&rsqb;, making a total of $&lsqb;total dollar amount of judgment&rsqb; that shall bear interest at the rate of &lsqb;rate of interest&rsqb;% a year.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
Plaintiff holds an equitable lien for the total sum superior to any claim or interest of defendants &lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT OWNER&rsqb; and &lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT LENDER&rsqb; on the following real property in &lsqb;name of county&rsqb;, Florida:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
If the total sum with interest at the rate prescribed in paragraph 1 and all costs of this action accruing subsequent to this judgment are not paid, the clerk of this court shall sell the property at public sale on &lsqb;date of sale&rsqb;, between 11:00 a.m. and 2:00 p.m., to the highest bidder for cash, except as prescribed in paragraph 4, at the &lsqb;location of sale&rsqb; door of the courthouse in &lsqb;name of county&rsqb; in accordance with st.ref.id="I03RVZV">Section 45.031, Florida Statutes. The clerk of this court shall receive the service charge pursuant to <field>st.ref.id="I03HNOZ"</field>&sect;45.035, Fla. Stat. in making, recording, and certifying the sale and title that shall be assessed as costs.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
Plaintiff shall advance all subsequent costs of this action and shall be reimbursed for them by the clerk if plaintiff is not the purchaser of the property at the sale. If plaintiff is the purchaser, the clerk shall credit plaintiff's bid with the total sum with interest and costs accruing subsequent to this judgment, or such part of it, as is necessary to fully pay the bid.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
After filing the certificate of title the clerk shall distribute the proceeds of the sale, as far as they are sufficient, by paying: first, plaintiff's costs; second, documentary stamps affixed to the certificate; third, plaintiff's attorney fees; fourth, the total sum due plaintiff, less the items paid, plus interest from this date to the date of the sale; and shall retain any remaining amount for subsequent distribution pursuant to st.ref.id="I03HNNR">&sect;45.031 Fla. Stat.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
IF THIS PROPERTY IS SOLD AT PUBLIC AUCTION, THERE MAY BE ADDITIONAL MONEY FROM THE SALE AFTER PAYMENT OF PERSONS WHO ARE ENTITLED TO BE PAID FROM THE SALE PROCEEDS PURSUANT TO THIS FINAL JUDGMENT.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
IF YOU ARE A SUBORDINATE LIENHOLDER CLAIMING A RIGHT TO FUNDS REMAINING AFTER THE SALE, IF ANY, YOU MUST FILE A CLAIM WITH THE CLERK NO LATER THAN THE DATE THAT THE CLERK REPORTS THE FUNDS AS UNCLAIMED. IF YOU FAIL TO FILE A TIMELY CLAIM, YOU WILL NOT BE ENTITLED TO ANY REMAINING FUNDS.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
On filing the certificate of title defendants and all persons claiming under or against defendants since the filing of the notice of lis pendens shall be foreclosed of all estate in or claim to the property and the purchaser at the sale shall be let into possession of the property.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|33|10:33">
<form.text>
Jurisdiction of this action is retained to enter further orders as are proper including, without limitation, writs of possession.

<form.text>
See cc.ref.id="I03TKZT">State ex rel. Ervin v. Smith, 160 So. 2d 518 (Fla. 1964). When judgment is for defendant, the action is dismissed. See <x>&sect;10:18. The commencement in this action omits the reference to the presentation of evidence even though it is a nonjury form. This is so because an issue of fact in prohibition is virtually impossible. See <x>&sect;10:73 (for the writ). This is a review action so the appellate rules govern. See <field>st.ref.id="I0359XP"</field>Fla. R. App. P. 9.100(f).
</x>
</form.text>
</form>
</section.body>
</section>

This action was tried before the court on all issues, except compensation for the way of necessity. The court finds that plaintiff is entitled to a statutory way of necessity because plaintiff's property, described hereinafter, is outside any municipality, is used for agricultural purposes and has no practicable route of egress or ingress to the nearest practicable public or private road. Pursuant to the verdict rendered in this action on compensation, the court hereinafter adjudicates the amount of compensation for the way of necessity. On the evidence presented
</form.text>

<form.text>
YOU ARE COMMANDED to summon garnishee <inline.instr>&lsqb;NAME OF GARNISHEE&rsqb;</inline.instr> to serve an answer to this writ on <inline.instr>&lsqb;name of plaintiff's attorney&rsqb;</inline.instr>, plaintiff's attorney, whose address is <inline.instr>&lsqb;address of plaintiff's attorney&rsqb;</inline.instr>, and to file the original with the clerk of this court either before service on the attorney or immediately thereafter, stating:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.unit>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
whether defendant &lsqb;NAME OF DEFENDANT&rsqb;is employed by garnishee, and
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
if so, the gross amount of periodic payments of salary or wages payable to defendant, and
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
the pay period for defendant, and requiring garnishee to withhold from each payment due or coming due of defendant's salary or wages after the service of this writ the amount exceeding:
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(a)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
&lsqb;text dollar amount of weekly amount&rsqb; dollar if defendant is paid weekly;
</form.text>
</form.para>
</form.item>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(b)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
&lsqb;text dollar amount of bi-weekly amount&rsqb; dollar if defendant is paid bi-weekly;
</form.text>
</form.para>
</form.item>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(c)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
&lsqb;text dollar amount of semi-monthly amount&rsqb; dollar if defendant is paid semi-monthly; or
</form.text>
</form.para>
</form.item>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(d)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
&lsqb;text dollar amount of monthly amount&rsqb; dollar if defendant is paid monthly; and
</form.text>
</form.para>
</form.item>
<form.item>
<name.block>
<designator>(e)</designator>
</name.block>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
in addition to the above amount withheld, garnishee may retain up to $&lsqb;dollar amount of retention&rsqb; for the first deduction and $&lsqb;dollar amount of subsequent retentions&rsqb; for each subsequent deduction for administrative expenses.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
BUT IN NO EVENT to withhold more than 25% of the gross salary or wages of defendant after deducting Social Security and income withholding taxes. If defendant is the head of a family residing in Florida, no amount shall be withheld unless the defendant has signed a statutory waiver and earns more than $750 a week. The head of a family is a person who is providing more than one-half of the support for a child or other dependent. If defendant claims to be the head of a family, garnishee shall notify defendant to seek an exemption from this writ and to consult an attorney about the exemption.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
Otherwise, withholding shall continue until plaintiff's judgment in the sum of $&lsqb;dollar amount of judgment&rsqb; is satisfied or defendant's employment by garnishee terminates or the further order of this court. Withheld payments shall be retained by garnishee until the further order of this court.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
A failure to comply with this writ may result in garnishee paying the garnished amounts twice and in garnishee being held in contempt of court.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
ORDERED at &lsqb;name of city&rsqb;, Florida on &lsqb;date of garnishment&rsqb;.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
in addition to the above amount withheld, garnishee may retain up to $&lsqb;dollar amount of retention&rsqb; for the first deduction and $&lsqb;dollar amount of subsequent retentions&rsqb; for each subsequent deduction for administrative expenses.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
BUT IN NO EVENT to withhold more than 25% of the gross salary or wages of defendant after deducting Social Security and income withholding taxes. If defendant is the head of a family residing in Florida, no amount shall be withheld unless the defendant has signed a statutory waiver and earns more than $750 a week. The head of a family is a person who is providing more than one-half of the support for a child or other dependent. If defendant claims to be the head of a family, garnishee shall notify defendant to seek an exemption from this writ and to consult an attorney about the exemption.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
Otherwise, withholding shall continue until plaintiff's judgment in the sum of $&lsqb;dollar amount of judgment&rsqb; is satisfied or defendant's employment by garnishee terminates or the further order of this court. Withheld payments shall be retained by garnishee until the further order of this court.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
A failure to comply with this writ may result in garnishee paying the garnished amounts twice and in garnishee being held in contempt of court.
</form.text>
</form.para>
<form.para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|69|10:69">
<form.text>
ORDERED at &lsqb;name of city&rsqb;, Florida on &lsqb;date of garnishment&rsqb;.
</form.text>
</form.para>

<section.front>
<outline.name.block>
<label>&sect;</label>
<designator>10:75</designator>
<name>Final disposition form</name>
</outline.name.block>
<online.view>
<online.view.item>Author's Comment</online.view.item>
</online.view>
</section.front>
<section.body>
<para ct.id="3d29be30775711ee8e1ba9ecff0bf883|75|10:75">
<para.text>
See st.ref.id="I048OIS">Fla. R. Civ. P. 1.545. The Supreme Court adopted <trace></trace>Form 1.998 in civil procedure and <trace></trace>Form 12.999 in family procedure. The appropriate form must be filed by the plaintiff or petitioner in family actions and by the prevailing party in civil actions when the matter is finally disposed of. The clerk files it for a pro se party or when the action is dismissed for lack of prosecution.
</para.text>
</para>
</section.body>
